**Including "LIVE NOW" in Titles:**

- **Pros:**

[2025-03-05 20:51:07] ChatGPT:
îˆƒIn light of Whatnot's updated Surprise Products Policy, effective March 10, 2025, it's essential to align your sales strategies with these new guidelines to ensure compliance and maintain buyer trust.îˆ„ îˆ€citeîˆ‚turn0search0îˆîˆ†

**Key Policy Highlights:**

- **Transparency:** îˆƒAll surprise products must be opened and shown during the livestream, with contents visible and kept on screen throughout the show.îˆ„îˆ†

- **Pricing Disclosure:** îˆƒSellers are required to list the floor price (minimum value), ceiling price (maximum value), average price, and the number of items included in the surprise product.îˆ„îˆ†

- **Prohibited Practices:** îˆƒRandomization through physical machines (e.g., vending machines, raffle drums) is not permitted. Additionally, inflating the market value of items is strictly prohibited.îˆ„îˆ†

**Recommendations for Compliance:**

1. **Transition to Autoboxes:** îˆƒShift from Virtual Pull Boxes to Autoboxes with clearly defined contents. This approach aligns with Whatnot's emphasis on transparency and allows buyers to know exactly what they're purchasing.îˆ„îˆ†

2. **Detailed Descriptions:** îˆƒProvide comprehensive information about each Autobox, including:îˆ„îˆ†
